NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION (1) OF SECTION (15) OF THE TAMIL NADU HIGHWAYS ACT, 2001.
(LA-V(2)/ 11212805 /2025)
No. VI(1)/517(c-1)/2025.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the Schedule below have to be 
acquired for the Highways Purpose for the Construction of “Widening from two lane paved shoulder to four lane 
at Km 34/0 – 38/2 of Avinashi – Mettupalayam Road” in Bellepalayam, Karamadai & Sikkadhasampalayam Villages, 
Mettupalayam Taluk & Coimbatore District and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to 
be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by the Chief Engineer, (Highways) 
Constructions and Maintenance Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the 
Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 15 of the Tamil Nadu Highways Act, 2001 (Tamil Nadu Act 34 of 2002), the 
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below measuring an total extent of 
974.50 Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for the purpose for the Construction of “Widening from 
two lane paved shoulder to four lane at Km 34/0 – 38/2 of Avinashi – Mettupalayam Road” in Bellepalayam, 
Karamadai & Sikkadhasampalayam Villages, Mettupalayam Taluk & Coimbatore District.
The Plan of the lands are kept in the Office of the Special District Revenue Officer (LA), Highways in Coimbatore 
may be inspected on any day during office hours.
